Li talons est aucune fois esmeus, et aucune fois desaluez plenement, et dedens et defuer.	The heels are never misaligned, and never completely dislocated, inside and out.
Et li signes si est que li cheville est enflee, et tent avant a la partie ou elle est desaluee: li ramenemens si est legier, et le doit on estendre legierement a ses mains quant il est esmeus soulement.	And the signs are that the ankle is dislocated, and it bends before the part where it is dislocated: with slight movements, we bring it to our hands when it is only slightly misaligned.
Et quant il est desaluez dou tot, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et le tigne I ministres fors par la jambe, desus la cheville; puis trai le piet a toi a ta main destre, et puis a la senestre II fois, puis l’estent en haut, et boute bellement lou piet en haut; et fai ce II fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet; s’elle revient, c’est bien; se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient; et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche I passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide; puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a I liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet; puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent; puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.	And when it is completely dislocated from the top, you must put the patient upright, and stretch the leg away from them, over the ankle; then bring the foot to your right hand, and then to your left twice, then raise it up, and push it down firmly; and do this twice, as we said, by pushing and pulling the foot: if it returns, it is good; if not, start again with the treatment, because it will return; and if it cannot return like this, make the patient lie on his back on the ground, and place a rod firmly between his thighs, and tie the sheets so that he does not fall; then stretch the leg healthy at its end, and others ministers extends the foot in their hands or at the leg, that they keep the foot when you extend it; then put the surgeon equal to the dislocation in their hands, and others ministers stretch the healthy leg away from them, and the dislocation will return completely.
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois; puis le laisse II jors ou III, et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain; puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par IIII jors; et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	And when it is well done, so that the plaster and the staves are formed, and the foot is tied to the leg, and the strings that are behind the ankle are not too tight; then leave it II days or III, and let the strings become soft, if the brace; then take it off on the third day or fourth, and go to see the sick person after IV days; and if he goes forward this term, there is no danger that he will fall again.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if abscesses come out, so that you calm them down, as we have said elsewhere, as long as they are healthy.
des dois	of the two
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	When the two are dislocated, so that it is done well without work, and it is a light thing.
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus I leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne; et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a II chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse III jors, puis le deslie; et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the dislocations are not in any way at the back of the foot, so that you make the sick person sit on a plain bed or table all straight, and put your foot on what opens from these joints, then press your foot into form, as long as it recovers; and when it is even, and there is no opening, so set the sole of the foot on a table at two ends, then form the brace, and leave it III days, then take it off; and let him rest, as long as he is healthy.
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	of wound and dislocation together
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert: si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis; et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit; et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne; et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis; et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples; et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors.	When a wound comes with dislocation and you restore it, many times the patient dies: so do not be presumptuous in the cure, unless you are skilled in the art and have used it long, and unless you are compassionate and late to judge; do not be courageous. And use at first soothing things for an abscess, and leave the patient with God, if you see no hope of health; and when you see hope, now restore the limb to its place, so that the abscesses come; and when the limbs are in their places, administer dry things, and cure the wound as it should be, with the ointments we have said for simple diseases; and do not enter a path of fear, according to what I have said, because this will bring you to ruin according to your Creator, and for the sake of arming and protecting yourself and your body.
Amen	Amen
